---
layout: "post"
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus In Agda"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory, home
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code was tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed in the seminar of logic at Universidad EAFIT.

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2069" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Bound"></a><a id="2076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Module">Bound</a> <a id="2082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2083" class="Bound">Type</a> <a id="2088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2090" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="2093" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2095" class="Keyword">where</a>

Syntax using indexes.

      <a id="3195" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3115" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1514" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3205" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3208" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1434" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3106" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3211" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3108" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2453" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3106" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3110" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

      <a id="3284" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3286" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3264" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3288" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3248" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="3293" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3251" class="Bound">t₁&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4297" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5919" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5922" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5924" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2623" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5912" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5934" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5936" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5939" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1344" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5947" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5953" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="5988" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5990" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="5994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4440" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="5998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5998" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="6000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4440" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5922" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1490" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="6011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5939" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="6015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5998" class="Bound">t</a><a id="6016" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6710" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5298" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6684" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6747" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6752" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6754" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6759" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6782" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6784" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6759" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6804" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6809" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6811" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6816" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6817" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6819" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6822" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6827" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6836" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6838" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6568" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6816" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7069" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7081" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7083" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7084" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7085" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7091" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7094" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7096" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2623" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7084" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7106" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7112" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7114" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7115" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7117" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1469" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7125" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7133" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4440" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7141" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4440" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7146" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7094" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7115" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2749" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7141" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7157" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7163" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8689" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8770" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8776" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8779" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1469" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8789" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8791" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8793" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8794" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8796" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8798" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7069" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8810" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8779" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8814" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8817" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2398" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8824" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8770" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8834" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8836" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8837" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8838" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8840" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8842" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8849" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8837" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8860" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10491" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10557" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9960" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10565" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9960" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9894" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10574" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10581" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10597" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9483" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10612" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9483" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10627" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10629" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9483" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10641" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10675" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10708" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10740" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10828" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10876" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
